Dear ferret users,

I have a file of data file which contains gridded SST data(401x301) and i want to read that file using standard ascii reading procedure following examples in ferret documentation. Problem is only first row is being read and others are ignored by ferret. Herewith i have attached the ascii file i have used and the ferret script to read it. Hope someone respond to my query.   Thank in advance.

yes? go regrid.jnl
define axis/x=1:401:1  xaxis
define axis/y=1:301:1  yaxis
define grid/x=xaxis/y=yaxis     mygrid
file/grid=mygrid/format=delimited/delimiter="\,"/var=sst/columns=401  sst_281.csv
set var/bad=-9999 sst
save/file=test.cdf/clobber   sst
 LISTing to file test.cdf

yes? can var/all; use test.cdf ; sh da
 
    1> ./test.cdf  (default)
 name     title                             I         J         K         L         M         N
 SST      SST                              1:401     1:1       ...       ...       ...       ...


regards..
